Method	:	POST

{
        "airport_group_name"        :        "Sampple",
        "account_type_id"                :        "2",
        "account_id"                        :        "42",
        "airport_check"                        :        {"all_airport":"Y","selected_airport":"Y"},
        "airport_info"                        :        {"CA":"YYZ,YVR,YHU","IN":"ALL_AIRPORT","SG":"ALL_AIRPORT"},
        "status"                                :        "A"
}
